T43n1830_03a:0311c04_8_0 或遮餘部至互為因緣。 "Sometimes, other schools are rejected as causes and conditions for their mutual existence.
T43n1830_03a:0311c04_8_0 述曰。 The Commentary explains:
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 薩婆多等以善色望四蘊為因。 The Sarvāstivādins consider good visible matter to be the cause of the four aggregates.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 四望色蘊亦得為因　此即不然。 The four aggregates can also be the cause of the four visible matters. This is not possible.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 唯引自果因果隨順。 They refer only to their own effect, and cause and effect follow each other.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 功能同故名為因緣。 Because their function is the same, they are called causes and conditions.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 若增上緣等。 If it were a dominant condition, etc.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 義則可爾。 In this sense, it is possible.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 如何色等與心為因。 How can form, etc., be the cause of mind?
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 不相隨順功能異故。 Because they are not mutually conformable and because their function is different.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 問言恒隨轉名為種子。 Question: It is called seed that constantly evolves.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 第八識現行既恒隨轉。 The present eighth consciousness is constantly evolved.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 為名種不　有說亦得。 Is it called seed? According to some, it is also possible.
T43n1830_03a:0311c11_1_0 以名一切種子識故　若謂然者。 Because it is called the consciousness that embraces all the seeds. If you say that this is so, then what is the reason?
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 此現行望自種既非因緣。 This presently functioning seed is not a cause and condition.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 非能熏故如何名種　有說不得。 Since it is not capable of perfuming, how can it be called seed?
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 言一切種子識。 Some say that it cannot be called the consciousness that contains all the seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 含藏一切法能生一切法名一切種。 It contains all the factors that are able to engender all the factors and is called the "whole seeds."
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 非彼現行能生自種。 It is not that which is able to engender its own seed in the present.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 種雖依識現行自體。 Although seed depends on the actual consciousness, it is its own essence.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 是識所緣。 It is the object of consciousness.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 不同於識。 Therefore, it is different from consciousness.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 故識現行非名種子　此闕何義也　與果不俱故　其無性人第七識亦具六義。 Therefore, the actual consciousness that functions is not called the seed. What is the meaning of this incomplete statement? Because it is not simultaneous with the result. The seventh consciousness, which has no self-essence, also possesses six meanings.
T43n1830_03a:0311c18_2_0 應名種子　此亦不然。 It should therefore be called the seed. This is also not possible.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 論自解言與現行果俱現和合方成種子。 The Discourse says, "The seed is formed only when it is combined with the actual result.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 種子之法其相沈隱。 The characteristics of the seed are profound and obscure.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 所生果法其相麁顯。 The characteristics of the result that is produced are gross and obvious.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 故與現俱方成種子。 Therefore, it is only when it is combined with the actual result that it is formed as a seed.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 第七相顯。 The seventh characteristic is evident.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 設所熏種。 Suppose the seed that is perfumed.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 果乃沈隱。 The result is profound and obscure.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 不與現行果法和合。 It is not formed by the actual result.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 不名種子。 It is not called the seed.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 第八現識亦然。 The same applies to the present consciousness of the eighth.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 無所生果故。 Because there is no result that is produced.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 第八門中以上明種。 In the eighth gate, the above explains the seed.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 自下第三總結聊簡。 The third section below summarizes briefly.
T43n1830_03a:0311c23_11_0 論。 Discussion:
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 唯本識中至成種非餘。 In the fundamental consciousness only seeds are formed.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 述曰。 Comment:
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 簡上轉識等非名種義。 The above-mentioned transformation of consciousness and so on is not the meaning of names and seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 此中別解上六義中。 Here I explain separately the above-mentioned six meanings.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 言唯內種具有六義。 It is said that only internal seeds have six meanings.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 然世親攝論亦通外種。 Nevertheless, the Shiqin gathering lun also refers to external seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 此中引之解。 Here I cite an interpretation.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 外穀麥種既能生果。 Since seeds of grain and wheat can produce fruits, are they called seeds?
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 名種子不。 Answer:
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 論。 The Discourse says:
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 外穀麥等至非實種子。 "External grain and wheat, etc., are not real seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 述曰。 Comment:
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 雖識所變假名種子。 Even though they are what is transformed by consciousness, they are false names and seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 非實種子。 They are not real seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a01_10_0 現行法故　攝大乘云。 Because they are actual entities, they are included in the Mahāyāna.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 作．不作失．得過。 What is done, what is not done, and what is gained are contradictory.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 故成相違。 Therefore, it is established that they are contradictory.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 外種內為緣。 External seeds take internal conditions as conditions.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 由依彼熏習。 It is because they depend on perfuming.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 又引頌云。 Furthermore, quoted from the verse:
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 天．地．風．虛空。 Heaven, earth, wind, and empty space.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 波．池．方．大海。 Wave, a pond, a square, and the ocean.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 皆真內所作。 They are all truly produced internally.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 分別不在外　故由內種。 Differentiation does not reside externally. Therefore, it is caused by internal seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 外穀等熟彼非實種　問種亦識所變。 External grains, etc., that ripen are not real seeds." Question: "The seeds too are consciously transformed.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 應非實種子　答曰不然。 Should they not be real seeds?" Answer: "No, they are not.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 內種識變已復生麥等。 After the internal seeds have consciously transformed, wheat, etc., are reborn.
T43n1830_03a:0312a06_17_0 麥等復識變。 Wheat, etc., also consciously transform.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 以重變故。 Because they repeatedly change.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 故非種子。 Therefore, they are not seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 如眼根等。 They are like the organ of sight, etc.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 故下文云。 That is why the following passage says:
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 外麥等剋體。 External wheat, etc., overcomes its substance.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 非因緣生果。 It is not the result that arises from causes and conditions.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 故因緣唯內種。 Therefore, causes and conditions are only internal seeds.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 非外種故　此等已上並攝論有。 Because they are not external seeds. The above mentioned topics are all included in the present treatise.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 自下第九雙辨內外生．引二因。 The following ninth pair distinguishes internal and external arising and introduces two causes.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 此內外種皆有生．引二因體不。 Are these internal and external seeds able to have arising and introduce the substance of two causes?
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 答有。 Answer: Indeed.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 何者。 What is this?
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 論。 The Discourse says:
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 此種勢力至即名引因。 When the power of this seed reaches, it is called the guiding cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312a13_9_0 述曰。 The Commentary explains:
T43n1830_03a:0312a19_10_0 其內外種生近果生正果名生因。 # <br/>引遠果引殘果名引因　無性云。 # <br/>如內識種生現識等名近果。 # <br/>是生因。 # <br/>望名色等是遠果。 # <br/>是引因。 # <br/>外種望芽是近果。 # <br/>是生因。 # <br/>望莖等是遠果。 # <br/>是引因　天親云。 # <br/>如內種子生正果名生因。 # <br/>生殘果名引因。 # <br/>即現在種生現在身名生因。 The internal and external seeds give rise to the immediate result and give rise to the real result. This is called the generating cause. # <br/>To project a distant result and to project a remnant result is called the generating cause. # <br/>The Ārūpyas say, "As the seeds of internal consciousness give rise to present consciousness, etc., this is called the immediate result. # <br/>This is the generating cause. # <br/>Looking at names and forms, etc., this is the distant result. # <br/>This is the generating cause. # <br/>External seeds look at sprouts and this is the immediate result. # <br/>This is the generating cause. # <br/>Looking at stems, etc., this is the distant result. # <br/>This is the generating cause." Tianxin said, "As the internal seeds give rise to the real result, this is called the generating cause. # <br/>The producing remnant result is called the generating cause. # <br/>The present seeds that give rise to the present body are called the generating cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312a26_5_0 生六處等皆名生因。 # <br/>引餘枯喪屍骸等名引因　雖生他界等。 # <br/>勢分力故餘骸尚有。 # <br/>如下自解。 # <br/>外種生芽莖等為生因。 # <br/>是正因。 # <br/>生枯死時草等。 # <br/>是引因。 # <br/>勢分力故。 # <br/>然至此位時。 # <br/>內外種皆無。 # <br/>或生他界等。 # <br/>或種已久滅。 # <br/>然由前生勢分力故引彼猶有。 The six bases of existence, etc., are all referred to as the generating cause. # <br/>Even though they are reborn in other realms, etc., other bodies exist because of the power of their divisions. # <br/>The following passage explains: # <br/>External seeds that produce sprouts, stems, etc., are the generating cause. # <br/>This is the correct cause. # <br/>When they are born, when they die, grass, etc. # <br/>This is the generating cause. # <br/>Because of the power of their divisions. # <br/>However, when they reach this state, internal and external seeds do not exist. # <br/>Sometimes they are reborn in other realms, etc. # <br/>Sometimes the seeds have long since disappeared. # <br/>However, by virtue of the power of the power of their previous birth, they are attracted and still exist.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 即義說彼生因之種名引因　然今兩說生．引二因俱無別體。 According to the same principle, the seed that is the cause of arising is called the projecting cause. However, we now speak of the two causes of arising and the projecting cause. There is no separate entity.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 一體望別故說二也。 Since they are one in essence, they are said to be two.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 若無引因勢分力者。 If there is no power of the projecting cause, it is impossible.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 一切死後皆應頓絕如化生死。 After death, all apparitional births and deaths should suddenly cease.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 若遍四生具二因者。 If the four types of apparitional births are supplied with the two causes, then there is no nature.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 無性理勝。 The principle is superior.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 以化生死無屍骸故。 Because apparitional births and deaths have no corpse.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 然世親論意。 Nevertheless, the meaning of Vasubandhu's discussion is this:
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 無著大師為成引因說枯喪等。 Wuzhuang, the great teacher, explained dried-up and so on for the sake of the accomplishment of the projecting cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 故說頌言。 Therefore, verses are spoken of:
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 枯喪由能引。 dried-up and so on because they are able to project.
T43n1830_03a:0312b02_9_0 如任運後滅。 It is just as when one dies spontaneously.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 天親解云。 The Discourse on the Extinction of Devasubha says:
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 若無引因。 If there is no guiding cause, there will be no result.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 應無枯喪果如任運後滅。 There will be no depletion, just as it ceases spontaneously.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 但是天親解略。 It is just that the Discourse on the Extinction of Devasubha summarizes.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 無性釋廣。 The Explanation on the Nonexistence of Nature extensively explains.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 亦不相違。 There is no contradiction either.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 此雖攝論文。 Although this treatise gathers all these texts, it does not go beyond them.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 然對法第四卷說能引．所引能生．所生。 Nevertheless, in the fourth fascicle of the Abhidharmasamuccaya we speak of the guiding cause, the generating cause, and the generating cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 瑜伽第九說能引．所引俱是引因。 In the ninth chapter of the Yogacarabhumi it is said that the guiding cause and the generating cause are simultaneously the guiding cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 能生名生因。 The generating cause is called the generating cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 瑜伽第十云。 In the tenth chapter of the Yogacarabhumi it is said:
T43n1830_03a:0312b08_14_0 從無明乃至受是引因。 From ignorance up to feeling are the guiding causes.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 愛．取．有是生因　此意欲顯未潤七支去果猶遠名為引因。 Craving, grasping, and existence are the causes of arising. The intention here is to show that the seven parts that have not yet been nourished go far away from the result.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 引遠果故。 Because they lead to a distant result.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 能潤二支．及所潤有。 They nourish the two parts and nourish the existences.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 去果近故名曰生因。 Because they go far away from the result, they are called the causes of arising.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 近生果故。 Because they give rise to a result when they are near.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 亦即此中近．遠所攝。 In this same sense, they are included in the list of near and distant.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 無性但約已潤種中果去因為近．遠。 There is no nature; it is simply that the fruit in the seed that has already been nourished is near and distant from the cause.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 瑜伽約潤．未潤位去果近．遠。 The yoga treats the state of having been nourished as being near and distant from the result.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 亦不相違。 Neither is there any contradiction.
T43n1830_03a:0312b14_3_0 次第十四緣分別辨內外種因．非因緣。 The fourteen conditions in succession distinguish between internal and external causes and conditions that are not causes and conditions.
T43n1830_03a:0312b20_9_0 熏．不熏別。 permeation is distinct from non-permeation.

T43n1830_03a:0312b20_9_0 述曰。 The comment says:
T43n1830_03a:0312b20_9_0 無性攝大乘第二卷說。 The teaching on the nonexistence of nature is given in the second fascicle of the Mahāyāna school.
T43n1830_03a:0312b20_9_0 如從其炭．牛糞．毛等。 It is just as charcoal, cow dung, hair, etc.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 如次生巨勝．青蓮根．及蒲。 In this way, the seeds of giant lotuses, blue lotus roots, and pomegranate trees arise one after another.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 非巨勝等與炭等。 It is not that giant lotuses, etc., are the same as charcoal.

T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 俱生俱滅由熏習故生香氣等。 Because of permeation, fragrance, etc., arise.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 名有熏習。 This is called the permeation of existence.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 外種不定。 External seeds are not determined.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 內則定熏　故外種子既唯現行。 Since internal seeds are definitely permeated, external seeds are only active.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 為增上緣辨所生果。 They are the dominant condition for distinguishing the result that is to be produced.
T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 論。 The Discourse says:

T43n1830_03a:0312b26_4_0 述曰。 The Commentary explains:

T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 從內共相種子生故。 Because they arise from the seeds of the internal common characteristics.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 如攝大乘自廣分別。 Thus it is explained in detail in the Collection of the Great Vehicle.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 自下第二解熏習義。 The following is the second explanation of the meaning of permeation.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 於中有三。 There are three items here.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 初總問。 The first is a general question.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 次略答。 The second is an abbreviated answer.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 後廣辨。 I will discuss them at length later.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 論。 Discourse:
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 依何等義立熏習名。 What is the meaning of the term permeation?
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 述曰。 My explanation is:
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 初問起也。 The first question arises.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 論。 Discourse:
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 所熏能熏至故名熏習。 Permeation is what perceives and reaches. Therefore, it is called permeation.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 述曰。 My explanation is:
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 此標具義。 This represents the complete meaning.
T43n1830_03a:0312c03_14_0 釋熏習名。 The term permeation is given to explain the name of permeation.

T43n1830_03a:0326b09_11_0 何故此識不緣無為　若實無為因未證故。 Why is it that this consciousness does not take unconditioned things as its object? Because the true unconditioned cause has not yet been realized.
